Suite can open a wide variety of file formats.\r\n\r\n- Opening text documents\r\nIn addition to OpenDocument formats (.odt, .ott, .oth, .odm, .sxw, .stw, and .sxg ), Word Editor can open the .wks, and .123)\r\n• Data Interchange Format (.dif)\r\n• Rich Text Format (.rtf)\r\n• Text CSV (.csv and .txt)\r\n• StarCalc formats (.sdc and .vor)\r\n• dBASE (.dbf)\r\n• SYLK (.slk)\r\n• Unified Office Format spreadsheet (.uos, .uof)\r\n• .htm and .html files, including Web page queries\r\n• Pocket Excel (pxl)\r\n• Quattro Pro 6.0 (.wb2)\r\n\r\n- Opening presentations\r\nIn addition to
